And on Warschauer Stra\xc3\x9fe in the heart of Friedrichshain-Kreuzberg - the district with the youngest population - students romp around prepared for funky nightlife. In Sch\xc3\xb6neberg, alternative lifestyles between culture and a vibrant nightlife find their home.\n</p><h2 class="MuiTypography-root makeStyles-header-266 makeStyles-fw-bold-269 MuiTypography-h6 MuiTypography-gutterBottom">Which district in Berlin is best connected? </h2><p class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-body1 MuiTypography-paragraph">In Berlin Mitte, you&#x27;re in the heart of Berlin and at the same time, you can leave the city in no time, as Berlin Hauptbahnhof is located here. You can look for a studio in a cheaper neighbourhood, and buy groceries in discount supermarkets and ahead.\\n\\n### Cost of living in Berlin for a family of 4\\n\\n\\u003E A family of 4 can expect to spend around \xe2\x82\xac4,665 per month to cover their living expenses, including rent. \\n\\nThe estimate includes an occasional meal in a restaurant and a cinema visit but does not account for childcare costs such as preschool or nursery.\\n\\n## Food Costs\\n\\n![Berlin cafe](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002FzzcHV722a9JUu4hlHb0sJ\\u002Ff5e52ce54d183049971c607d331504b6\\u002Ftoa-heftiba-6bKpHAun4d8-unsplash.jpg)\\n\\nFor international students or expats from [Germany](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002Fcountries\\u002FGermany)\'s neighbouring countries, groceries will be a paradise. And if you are an enrolled __student in Berlin, you can even get around for free!__ \\n\\n\\u003E Most [universities in Germany](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Funiversities-in-germany-for-international-students) are part of a network that provides students with __a semester ticket for a small fee__. \\n\\nThose, who don\'t have semseter tickets can buy one of the following __tickets or travel cards:__\\n\\n| Type     | Average cost   |\\n| ---------- | ---------- |\\n|Short trip ticket | \xe2\x82\xac3|\\n|Single tickets (2 hrs) | \xe2\x82\xac3|\\n|4-short-trip ticket| \xe2\x82\xac6|\\n|24-hour ticket| \xe2\x82\xac8.80|\\n|4-trip ticket| \xe2\x82\xac9.40|\\n|7-day ticket | \xe2\x82\xac36.00 |\\n|School student monthly ticket | \xe2\x82\xac77,50 |\\n|Monthly ticket | \xe2\x82\xac86|\\n\\nFor most people in Berlin, __the BVG AB ticket of \xe2\x82\xac86 per month is the way to go.__ And if you plan to live not too far from your study or work, you can save some money by using a bike. It __starts at \xe2\x82\xac4.00__ with an extra __\xe2\x82\xac2.15__ being charged __per km.__\\n\\n## Leisure costs\\n\\n![Woman at a Museum](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F1ppkhQ7leWtQoi0qMCudwH\\u002Fdad0baabbc091cb4598f3f2af77d3be9\\u002FUntitled_design__2_.png)\\n\\nNow, on to the fun part of living: leisure. \\n\\n__This is roughly what you can expect to spend in your free time in Berlin:__\\n\\n| __Leisure time__    | __Average price__    |\\n| ---------- | ---------- |\\n| Lunch out (*meal including drink*)       | \xe2\x82\xac15       |\\n| Dinner out (*for 2 people*)       | \xe2\x82\xac28       |\\n| Theatre tickets (*for 1 person*)       | \xe2\x82\xac41.50       |\\n| Cinema tickets (*for 1 person*)       | \xe2\x82\xac10 (on some weekdays it\'s cheaper than on weekends!)       |\\n| Museum tickets | \xe2\x82\xac8 (but many nice galleries have free exhibitions)|\\n| Coffee (capuccino in a specialty coffee bar)      | \xe2\x82\xac3.50       |\\n\\n## Education costs\\n\\n![Student studying in the classroom](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F5jilV4L5wFXdJy6Rx754Qv\\u002Fcc843b70b5a16364fcd50639c682ede2\\u002Fphilippe-bout-93W0xn4961g-unsplash.jpg)\\n\\nYou\'ll be happy to hear that __[studying in Germany](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Fstudy-abroad-germany) is very affordable__. \\n\\nHere is the best news: __students with European residence permit don\'t pay tuition fees__ in __public institutions__ in Germany. Each semester you\'ll only be charged __semester fees__, which usually add up to __around \xe2\x82\xac300__.\\n\\nAnd if __you\'re coming from a country outside the EU__, you\'ll need to get a __residence permit__ before you arrive in Germany __to study for free__. Otherwise you can __expect to pay a tuition fee of \xe2\x82\xac1,500 per semester.__ But that\'s  still a gread deal cheaper than what you\'d pay in other European countries!\\n\\n## Health insurance costs\\n\\n![Health insurance information form](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F5SHXPD24kQEcUM0ZGLoghQ\\u002F068cfc32d722861ee98a468c25b59f6d\\u002FUntitled_design__3_.png)\\n\\nTo live in Germany you must take out a [health insurance](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Fhealth-insurance-in-germany). As an __international student__, you can expect to pay a discounted price of around __\xe2\x82\xac120 per month__ for public health insurance in Germany. \\n\\nIf you\'re a working professional, __a contribution of 7.3%__ will be taken from your __gross salary__.  The __maximum__ you can be charged is capped at __\xe2\x82\xac360 a month__.\\n\\n## There\'s space for any budget in Berlin\\n\\nJust about every lifestyle finds its home in Berlin. Students who try to live on a low student budget can certainly __keep their cost of living per month in Berlin small - even without missing out on that vibrant city vibe.__ Instead of spending your time (and money!) in one of those fancy cocktail bars, why not just sip beer from a *Sp\xc3\xa4ti* on the Weserstra\xc3\x9fe in [Neuk\xc3\xb6lln](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fdiscover-berlin-neuk\xc3\xb6lln) while soaking up the ease of Berlin? \\n\\nWith a sense for affordable alternatives, you can make it through life in Berlin with a cost of living __below \xe2\x82\xac1,011 per mont__h. \\n\\nExpats in Berlin that want to kick off their career in one of the hip [start-ups](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fstartups-in-berlin) can easily treat themselves to a dinner out, and go all in with the buzzling concerts and festivals. This central district of Berlin is pretty much __art heaven__!\\n\\nIf you\xe2\x80\x99re in Berlin for a semester to broaden your horizons, Mitte also boasts the impressive __Humboldt University__. This means that you\xe2\x80\x99ll find a lively student crowd and [nightlife scene](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fguide-to-berlin-nightlife) in this neighbourhood as well.\\n\\nIn case you\xe2\x80\x99re moving to Berlin to begin your professional career, you\xe2\x80\x99ll find that opportunities are abundant. As a true \\"pickpocket\'s paradise\\", Berlin Mitte __leads the crime statistics__ with a frequency of around 27,000 crimes per 100,000 inhabitants. \\n\\nHowever, if you look beyond petty crime, Berlin Mitte yet remains one of the safer neighbourhoods.\\n\\n### Rental Prices\\n\\nMitte is in the upper range of rental prices in Berlin with __an average price of \xe2\x82\xac13.87 per sq metre.__\\n\\n| __Type of accommodation__ | __Rental price__ |\\n| ---------- | ---------- |\\n| Room | \xe2\x82\xac550 |\\n| Apartment | \xe2\x82\xac1,500 |\\n\\n## 2. Lichtenberg\\n\\nLichtenberg is one of the most well-known neighbourhoods in East Berlin. Partly, because it\xe2\x80\x99s a prime example of the architecture of its post-Cold War days, made up of block-style concrete structures. Other reminders of the city\xe2\x80\x99s history exist here in the Stasi Museum, filled with spy memorabilia, and a former prison, now the Hohensch\xc3\xb6nhausen Memorial.\\n\\n![Berlin neighbourhoods](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F20EorWSn5A0U7JwopQ0eVX\\u002Fde43792cdad9ca33ba84caebf0c92e0d\\u002Fpavel-nekoranec-2NYswF8lZXU-unsplash.jpg)\\n\\n### Quality of Life\\n\\nDepending on your point of view, some young people see this area as hip, but others note that it\xe2\x80\x99s beginning to become outdated. __And since you\xe2\x80\x99re on the hunt for housing, lowering prices can work in your favour.__\\n\\nFamilies with kids will enjoy the green zones of Lichtenberg and one of Europe\xe2\x80\x99s largest zoos, Tierpark.\\n\\n__Lichtenberg also offers a wealth of business and [internship opportunities](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Finternships-in-berlin).__ Many private companies are taking advantage of the [budget-friendly](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002Fmoving-abroad-budgeting) pricing and are setting up shops in this area.\\n\\n### Infrastructure\\n\\nWhen you need to get around quickly in Berlin, the Berlin-Lichtenberg station offers a variety of links all across the city and beyond. So transportation is always fast and reliable.\\n\\n### Internationality\\n\\nThis quiet residential area is a multicultural hub. It\'s known for a __large Vietnamese community__ concentrated in the popular Dong Xuan Center. They share the neighbourhood with predominantly __working-class German families.__\\n\\n### Safety\\n\\nWhat\xe2\x80\x98s the safest district in Berlin? Ta-da: It\'s Lichtenberg! __With 9 461 crimes per 100,000 inhabitants, you\'re safer here than anywhere else in Berlin.__\\n\\n### Rental prices\\n\\nLichtenberg is not only the safest but also the cheapest neighbourhood in Berlin. __Its average rent cost index is \xe2\x82\xac9.03 per sq metre.__\\n\\n| __Type of accommodation__ | __Rental price__ |\\n| ---------- | ---------- |\\n| Room | \xe2\x82\xac470 |\\n| Apartment | \xe2\x82\xac820 |\\n\\n## 7. Tempelhof - Sch\xc3\xb6neberg\\n\\nLike so many of the cities in Berlin, [Tempelhof](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fdiscover-berlin-tempelhof-schoeneberg) played an important role during the Cold War with its now-defunct airport. Treptow - K\xc3\xb6penick\\n\\nTreptow and K\xc3\xb6penick are very popular Berlin neighbourhoods for young people and families, providing both safety and moderate housing prices. \\n\\n![Berlin neighbourhoods](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002FaGzYa4of4nl02Gzrdn1KB\\u002F6e1047cf4e46c657bd66f59ec294604f\\u002Fstefan-widua-OAGa7kxfDNY-unsplash.jpg)\\n\\n### Quality of Life\\n\\nThe older industrial buildings in Treptow are transforming into office spaces for startups or co-working, so you can expect __a young crowd of professionals.__ That brings along plenty of __nightlife options and an inspiring art scene.__ At the same time, the tranquillity of __K\xc3\xb6penick\xe2\x80\x99s forests, lakes, and nature preserves__ makes the area perfect for __windsurfing, sailing and cycling.__ \\n\\nThe popular __Treptower Park__ offers a great place for __picnics with friends and outdoor family activities.__ And it\'s also home to Archenhold Observatory, a favourite stop for science and astrology students. __Plus, it\xe2\x80\x99s a great place to see Berlin\xe2\x80\x99s skyline.__\\n\\n### Infrastructure\\n\\nTreptow is close to Kreuzberg, Friedrichshain, and Neuk\xc3\xb6lln, and frequent trains make it simple to get around.\\n\\nK\xc3\xb6penick is a little further away from the centre of Berlin. But, just like Spandau, it\xe2\x80\x99s a quiet retreat close to the city via public transportation lines.\\n\\n### Internationality\\n\\nThanks to its low cost of living and its proximity to the hip areas of Kreuzberg and Neuk\xc3\xb6lln, __the Alt-Treptow neighbourhood is increasingly popular with young expats and creatives.__ The more you move to the east, the more family houses you\xe2\x80\x99ll encounter. \\n\\n__K\xc3\xb6penick isn\xe2\x80\x99t a particularly international district,__ but you\xe2\x80\x99ll still feel comfortable there as an expat.\\n\\n### Safety\\n\\nNo doubt about it: __with 9,623 cases per 100,000 inhabitants you are safer in Treptow - K\xc3\xb6penick than in nearly any other district.__ \\n\\n### Rental prices\\n\\nThe rents in Treptow-K\xc3\xb6penick roughly reflect the average rental prices in Berlin with __\xe2\x82\xac10 per sq meter.__\\n\\n| __Type of accommodation__ | __Rental price__ |\\n| ---------- | ---------- |\\n| Room | \xe2\x82\xac489 |\\n| Apartment | \xe2\x82\xac920 |\\n\\n## Not so obvious places to live in Berlin\\n\\n![bierpinsel](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F4mEzQgS7KrNWPS9I7qdtGf\\u002F0757dd0aa0fec3ddc68d604983fcded0\\u002Fpaul-g-xDA_ftU21P8-unsplash.jpg)\\n\\nWant to stay away from the action? In the popular districts of Berlin, it might be hard to find the piece and quiet you seek. Or maybe you\xe2\x80\x99re looking for a place to start a family. Then safety and nature might be your primary concerns.\\n\\nIf that sounds like you, consider the __tranquil residential areas of Steglitz - Zehlendorf, Marzahn - Hellersdorf, Reinickendorf, and Spandau.__\\n\\nEach of these districts lies on the outskirts of Berlin, bringing about all the benefits of suburban lifestyle. Here you can enjoy __the lowest rental prices and crime rates__ while having access to __beautiful recreational areas.__ Steglitz - Zehlendorf, Spandau, and Reinickendorf will treat you with lush forests and lakes. In Marzahn - Hellersdorf, you\xe2\x80\x99ll find historic GDR-era concrete towers, high-rise apartments and vast parks. \\n\\nAnd luckily Berlin\xe2\x80\x99s developed public transport infrastructure allows you to easily [commute](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Fcommuting-in-germany) to your study or work!\\n\\n| __Type of accommodation__ | __Rental price__ |\\n| ---------- | ---------- |\\n| Room | \xe2\x82\xac350- 469  |\\n| Apartment | \xe2\x82\xac900 - 1000 |\\n\\n![areal view on berlin](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F10ATJ9EhjcS88bH4KViDCu\\u002F459ca0406aef5d338455b14e27928d3a\\u002Fadrian-trinkaus-wlFtYjJEvR8-unsplash.jpg)\\n\\n## Let\xe2\x80\x99s recap\\n\\n__Urban families and expats with a higher income__ should consider the central location of __Berlin Mitte__ or the upper-middle-class hood of __Charlottenburg__.\\n\\nAre you looking for a hot spot for __culture and nightlife__? __Neuk\xc3\xb6lln, Friedrichshain, and Kreuzberg__ are easily the coolest areas in Berlin.\\n\\nIf you want to be surrounded by many __hip cafes and co-working spaces,__ look for an accommodation in __Pankow__. And in line with the simple economic principle of having more demand than supply, rental prices in Berlin have been skyrocketing in recent years. \\n\\nIn other words, \\n\\n\\u003E landlords in Berlin are spoilt for choice, competition in the housing market is tough. \\n\\nThe good news is that, despite strong competition, with HousingAnywhere, as an international, you\'ll still secure your accommodation before you arrive to [Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002Fs\\u002FBerlin--Germany)! Around the *Brandenburg Gate* you can literally feel the history; where once Prussian kings ruled you will now find a lot of elegant city villas, embassies and luxurious hotels. \\n\\nThat\'s not all! As we\'ve told you, Berlin-Mitte is a real tourist hotspot. You\'ll find *Tiergarten S\xc3\xbcd*, the government district and *Alexanderplatz* (\'*Alex*\'). \\n\\n__Did you know that Berlin Mitte was once part of East Berlin?__ If you pay attention to little details, you can spot even 30 years after the fall of the Wall whether you are in the former East or West of the city. For example, the lights are orange in the east and white in the west, even the traffic lights look different in the east! \\n\\n## New to Berlin-Mitte: What\'s going on off the beaten tourist track?\\nAsk true locals what they think of Berlin-Mitte and you\'ll no doubt get the same reaction: too expensive, too chic and too touristy. Art exhibition in an intimate bunker atmosphere\\nNo longer a massive refuge filled with fear and terror, __the Reichsbunker__ (aka *banana bunker* in GDR times) __today acts as a hub of inspiration and creativity__. In early 2000, Christian Boros bought the bunker and now exhibits his private collection of contemporary art. Amidst massive grey walls, you can admire works by international artists from 1990 to the present day. Among them are also alumni or professors of the [art universities of Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fart-universities-in-berlin): Ai Wei Wei, Olafur Eliasson or Tom\xc3\xa1s Saraceno\'s art pieces await you here.\\n\\nP.S. Not only does Berlin\'s largest church feature stained-glass windows in the chancel that stands out in the sunshine, but there\'s also a cosy setting below the church, in the crypt of the Hohenzollern dynasty. \\n\\nWhat\'s more: climbing up to the cupola walkway will reward you with a stunning view all over [Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany). \\n\\n![Discover Berlin-Mitte](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F3a1zzglrPS6kB9ofFQbW9v\\u002F08b5c6735526d4c92ec8373d1932e0f0\\u002Fgraes-magazine-lAD97nfMCTg-unsplash.jpg)\\n\\n### 3. There are even free concerts here on summer evenings. \\n\\n__For a bit of a royal feeling at breakfast, try the lemon caf\xc3\xa9 in K\xc3\xb6rnerpark__: surrounded by well-kept, delicate greenery, there are plenty of lemony things to discover here in the light-flooded garden house, but also tasty cakes. \\n\\n![K\xc3\xb6rnerpark Berlin](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F3gK5sLak9Rmh6GVGl7PVVe\\u002Fe14a35cebca273a293d1fa542003a97c\\u002Fgavin-mcgruddy-p23YJJMT16s-unsplash.jpg)\\n\\nOnce you\'re fully refreshed, turn left from K\xc3\xb6rnerpark and walk along Thomasstra\xc3\x9fe through Berlin\'s Schillerkiez district. Between Hermannstra\xc3\x9fe and Tempelhofer Feld, __the Schillerkiez in Berlin has an almost village-like atmosphere__ with a range of caf\xc3\xa9s, bars and restaurants unlike any other neighbourhood in Neuk\xc3\xb6lln. \\n\\nLet\'s move on to the next stop. Walk up Hermannstra\xc3\x9fe, turn right into Rollbergstra\xc3\x9fe and you\'ll almost see it: the KINDL - Centre for Contemporary Art.\\n\\n## 2. Kranoldplatz flea market__: Dive into the new and old treasures of Berlin. But if you are looking for a new desk or other second-hand furniture at one of the flea markets in Berlin, you might want to consider [Carsharing](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fgetting-around-in-berlin)!\\n\\n## Get free furniture in Berlin online\\nFree furniture in Berlin? Say no more! With a pinch of luck, you can even snatch furniture in Berlin for free! It\'s no secret though that when there\'s something for free, people speed up. That\'s why you shouldn\'t hesitate long and contact people directly. \\n\\n__On Facebook you have these groups for free furniture in Berlin:__\\n\\n- [Free Your Stuff Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fwww.facebook.com\\u002Fgroups\\u002Ffreeyourstuff\\u002F?fref=ts)\\n- [Sell Your Stuff Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fwww.facebook.com\\u002Fgroups\\u002Fsysberlin\\u002F)\\n- [M\xc3\xb6bel verkaufen, tauschen, verschenken](https:\\u002F\\u002Fwww.facebook.com\\u002Fgroups\\u002F218414381656724\\u002F) (German)\\n- [Zu Verschenken in Berlin & Brandenburg](https:\\u002F\\u002Fwww.facebook.com\\u002Fgroups\\u002F1455154191381889\\u002F) (German)\\n\\nSo, it\'s time to bring the Berlin vintage flair of understatement and casualness into your home!\\n\\n*Please reach out to content@housinganywhere.com if you have any suggestions or inquiries about the content on this page.*\\n","topicCluster":"livingIn"},{"title":"Expat Guide On How To Rent In Berlin","pathname":"\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Frent-in-berlin","content":"# Expat Guide On How To Rent In Berlin\\n\\nIf you\xe2\x80\x99re thinking [Germany](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002Fcountries\\u002FGermany) could be your new or temporary home, then [living in Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany) must have crossed your mind! After all, it\xe2\x80\x99s one of the [best cities in Germany](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Fbest-cities-in-germany-to-live)! \\n\\n![River Spree time laspe](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.ctfassets.net\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F7yej5sJqBhBqRxvfR2NivV\\u002Ffa27997860ae2a57706116023ca633e4\\u002FRiver_Spree_time_lapse.jpg)\\n\\n\\"Berlin is a young, fresh melting pot which never sleeps and where everything is possible. It almost feels as if the whole city were a start-up...\\", says HousingAnywhere\'s Max Zowodny from Berlin. So if you want to place yourself in the prime epicentre, \xe2\x80\x9cwhere things are happening\xe2\x80\x9d, Berlin can offer one of the most inspiring neighbourhoods in existence! \\n\\nAre you ready to learn all there is to know about renting in Berlin? Let\xe2\x80\x99s get started! This informative guide will help you understand all of the processes that are involved when you need to find a room in Berlin, including understanding your rental agreement, the documents that you\xe2\x80\x99ll need, how to find rental accommodation, which expat neighbourhoods to keep an eye on, and what to do after signing a rental contract.\\n\\n## Read up on German rental agreements to educate and protect yourself\\n\\nGiven that Berlin\xe2\x80\x99s __rental market is fiercely competitive__, it\xe2\x80\x99s good to __familiarise__ yourself with some __terms and tenant rights__. This way, when you see a rental contract, you\xe2\x80\x99ll know what to look out for. \\n\\n### What should I look out for in my rental agreement in Germany?\\n\\n![Signing a rental agreement](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.contentful.com\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F6FLA4fAqbXmiqPKwhh1rLQ\\u002F63010f93b76c90b03de86bc41d9ddcb9\\u002FSigning_a_rental_agreement_.jpg)\\n\\nA [rental agreement](http:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002Funderstanding-rental-agreements) is __always required__ when you are renting a room or an apartment in Germany. __A rental agreement not only protects the landlord but the tenant as well__.\\n\\n\\u003E If your landlord says that it isn\xe2\x80\x99t necessary, then insist upon getting one or begin to look for another property. \\n\\nThe __terminology__ in the rental agreement __can often be complex__; filled with legal jargon and may even be written in German. Resist the temptation to overlook the details and sign without reading through the contract thoroughly. __Don\xe2\x80\x99t be afraid to ask questions or seek legal guidance__ if there\xe2\x80\x99s anything in the contract you\xe2\x80\x99re uncertain about. Above all else, __never settle for a verbal agreement__ with a landlord; a __signed rental contract is essential__. \\n\\n\\u003EThe rental laws in Germany tend to be in favour of the tenant, so don\xe2\x80\x99t worry too much if you change your mind.\\n\\n__Most agreements contain standard components__ such as:\\n\\n- Personal details of both the tenant and the landlord, including phone number, address, and full name; pay special attention to how your name is spelt. \\n\\n- Address and description of the rental accommodation, including whether it is inclusive of utility bills [(*warmmiete*) or excluding (*kaltmiete*)](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Fwarm-rent-in-germany); inventory; and condition it must be left in.\\n\\n- Information regarding the length of the tenancy, the moving date, the moving out date. \\n\\n- Deposits and payment information- bank details, [when is the rent due](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Fpay-rent-germany), when can it increase, how much is the deposit, penalties for terminating early, and the possibility of extending the contract.\\n\\n- Additional terms and conditions for things like parking.\\n\\nIt\'s worth noting that it is __common practice__ for German landlords to ask for your __deposit to be paid immediately after signing__ the contract and __*before* moving in__. \\n\\nAnd while this may seem like a no-brainer, __make sure that everyone who will be living with you is included in the agreement__. Otherwise, you\xe2\x80\x99ll be solely responsible for rent payments, utilities and any remaining fees or money owed for damages to the property.\\n\\n## Get Your Documents in Order\\n\\nRemember that __finding a place to rent in Berlin is competitive__, so when you find something that fits your needs, it\xe2\x80\x99s __best to act as soon as possible__.\\n\\n\\u003E The [average rent in Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fcost-of-living-berlin) is \xe2\x82\xac552 for rooms and \xe2\x82\xac1086 for apartments. Use this as a benchmark to find housing in Berlin.\\n\\nBut as tempting as it is to start scrolling through Berlin homes for rent, ensure that you have all of your documentation ready. After all, you can\xe2\x80\x99t sign a rental agreement without these papers and you don\xe2\x80\x99t want any admin work being an obstacle to finding your dream house.\\n\\nTypically you will need the below documents to rent in Berlin:\\n\\n- A signed rental application form that you have received from the landlord or have downloaded online. \\n\\n- A copy of your residence permit (should it be required) and passport.\\n\\n- Proof of income for three months.\\n\\n- If applicable, a letter from a previous landlord stating you left the property in good condition and with no outstanding balances.\\n\\nIn Germany, landlords or real estate agents also like to __do a credit check before offering you a place to rent__. But the German credit check report (*SCHUFA*) is often sent to your German address. But since you don\xe2\x80\x99t yet have an address in Berlin, that is __a problem__. So make sure you prepare alternative reports to prove your financial health.\\n\\n## Finding Housing in Berlin\\n\\n![Student room in berlin](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.contentful.com\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F5vYSIdmCa9wD4ZJXo6ffqT\\u002F6c7d56c910b94d97f7c442c66ce7a356\\u002FStudent_room_in_berlin.jpg)\\n\\nThere\xe2\x80\x99re several ways to find both short term or long term rental in Berlin. __If you\xe2\x80\x99re a student, you can look for [student dormitories in Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Fstudent-accomodation-in-germany)__. But __such housing is limited__ and fills up very quickly. Nearly 60% of international students and all local students are forced to look specifically for rooms or apartments for rent in Berlin for students. \\n\\n![Rental apartment in Berlin](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.contentful.com\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F7hmsivGYjXKAiSYpP47i0v\\u002Fa888121b6fbf4699ce1935a549665626\\u002FRental_apartment_in_Berlin.jpg)\\n\\n__If you\xe2\x80\x99re an expat, you can look into rental agencies__ in Berlin; although their __fees are high__. Alternatively, you can browse through the __many groups and communities on Facebook__. However, __anyone can advertise on Facebook__ and because of the extremely competitive Berlin rental market, __you could easily be scammed__ under the pressure of booking something quickly.\\n\\nThis is why it\'s imperative that you take the time to do your research in __finding a reliable renting platform__ that is also __friendly to internationals__. By using *HousingAnywhere*:\\n\\n- Your rent will be protected for up to 48 hours after you\xe2\x80\x99ve moved in. This gives you time to assess the place and back out if necessary.\\n- You\xe2\x80\x99ll be protected from scammers with our machine learning backed scam-detection tech. \\n- You\xe2\x80\x99ll receive a refund and our help in case you\xe2\x80\x99re scammed. \\n- We\xe2\x80\x99ll help you beat your competition in finding places to rent in Berlin by sending email alerts based on your preferences .\\n\\n\\u003ETip: Understand how the [public transport works in Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fgetting-around-in-berlin) and see if your new rental is close to any public transport. This will make travelling to work, university, city centre, airport, or home that much easier. \\n\\n## Neighborhoods\\n\\n![Residential building Berlin](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.contentful.com\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F2xz7xQ3U37n3Z4onl0dgDZ\\u002F65c9c932722893bff3484671817bc551\\u002FResidential_building_Berlin.jpg)\\n\\n[Berlin\xe2\x80\x99s neighbourhoods](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fneighborhood-guide-Berlin) exhibit a sheer range of atmosphere; from the eccentric to the sleek, the city has a myriad of residential communities that can be historical, cultural, hip, artistic, modern, and techy.\\n\\nOf the 12 districts in Berlin, there are certain areas that appeal to international students and expats due to their proximity to universities, businesses, or large expat communities. Some neighbourhoods you may want to keep in mind include:\\n\\n1. Mitte\\n2. Neuk\xc3\xb6ln\\n3. Friedrichshain - Kreuzberg\\n4. Charlottenburg - Wilmersdorf \\n5. Pankow\\n6. Tempelhof - Sch\xc3\xb6neberg\\n7. Steglitz - Zehlendorf \\n\\n## Remember to register after you sign the contract\\n\\n![Rental apartment in Berlin](\\u002F\\u002Fimages.contentful.com\\u002Fqr8kennq1pom\\u002F1h2T60gSY6KlipBy0al62f\\u002F8b35d791a2acea1fd7a63dbe4e097dd0\\u002FRental_apartment_in_Berlin.jpg)\\n\\nOnce you find your dream room or apartment in Berlin, it\xe2\x80\x99s time to sign the contract! \\n\\nIf you __plan to stay in Berlin for over three months__, then __you\xe2\x80\x99ll need to [register your new address](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany\\u002Fregistration-in-berlin) with the B\xc3\xbcrgeramt (registration office)__ within 14 days of signing your rental agreement. \\n\\nRegistration is important as it will provide you with your tax identification number (*Steueridentifikationsnummer*) and your registration certificate. This will be necessary for things such as opening a [bank account](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Fgerman-bank-account-expats), [paying your rent](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Fpay-rent-germany), or [setting up your utilities](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FGermany\\u002Futilities-in-germany). \\n\\nThe registration offices tend to be extremely busy. To __prepare yourself for the long waiting list__ book your appointment as soon as you\xe2\x80\x99ve signed your rental agreement or schedule an appointment before signing the rental contract. \\n\\n## Get ready to live in Berlin!\\n\\nNow that you know the key steps to rent in Germany\xe2\x80\x99s capital \xe2\x80\x92 including the ins and outs of rental agreements, and how to find an apartment \xe2\x80\x92 you can relax and begin planning your [move to Berlin](https:\\u002F\\u002Fhousinganywhere.com\\u002FBerlin--Germany).
